                grid_type : 3,
                col_scroll_length   : 6,

            }
        }
    };

    (function () {
        if (utils.isMobile()) {
            var module = document.getElementById("new-grid-d42777");
            var game_specials = module.querySelectorAll(".col:not(.special) a.item.game_special");
            if (game_specials.length > 0) {
                for (var g = 0; g < game_specials.length; g++) {
                    game_specials[g].remove();
                }
                var cols = module.querySelectorAll(".col:not(.special)");
                var items = module.querySelectorAll(".col:not(.special) a.item");
                for (var c = 0; c < cols.length; c++) {
                    if (items.length > c * 2) {
                        cols[c].appendChild(items[c * 2]);
                        if (items.length > c * 2 + 1) {
                            cols[c].appendChild(items[c * 2 + 1]);
                        }
                    } else {
                        cols[c].parentElement.remove();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }());
    
    dg_init( obj );

</script>

</div>                    </div>
                            </div>
                <div class="clear"></div>
    </div>
</div>
